msg:We just returned from a brief stay at the Nuo Resort Hotel, which we chose in order to gain early entry into Universal Studios.  Wish we could have stayed longer!  We were pleasantly surprised at check-in by Wheeler, who let us know that we would be receiving a complementary room upgrade for our stay.  Next Damon escorted us to our lovely room and showed us around.  He also offered to connect with us on WeChat so that we could contact him at any time for assistance.  Every staff member we encountered in the hotel was very friendly and accommodating.  

We went to the spa and (in a lovely private suite) enjoyed very thorough foot massages.  My husband went back to the spa later for a full body massage and said it was really relaxing.  The atmosphere was very tranquil and luxurious.

We only ate breakfast in the hotel as we spent most of our time at Universal and CityWalk, but the restaurant where breakfast was served offered a nice variety of local and Western options.  I loved the egg station where your eggs are cooked to order.

Beautiful, elegant hotel, will definitely return if I have an opportunity!  Great place for Beijingers looking for a nice staycation.

As an undergraduate major in hotel management, I think NUO has done a good job in all aspects. When I visit Universal for the second time, I will continue to choose to stay.

msg:The NUO Resort Hotel is located on the south side of the entrance to Universal Studios. The hotel as a whole adopts the so-called New Orientalism. The architectural style, as far as the eye can see, is filled with a large number of vertical lines of bright copper/red copper/light ***** structures, as well as a tough combination of dry-hanging stone and open hard floors. The entire hotel lobby is almost like a luxury sales office... ...But I have to say, she is really beautiful, and she looks like a blockbuster in any photo she takes.
Free upgrade to a garden view room with a higher floor, including independent toilet, shower, bathtub, storage room (but unfortunately no entrance), double basins, independent sofa set + coffee table + simple tea set (black tea is not bad), and dressing room There is a table and tea bar (with coffee machine), free drinks in the refrigerator (the first round is free), the space is quite spacious, and living activities are very comfortable.
The mattress is moderately soft and hard, and the quilt's cotton feels good to the touch. Looking at the carpets, curtains, pillows, towels, etc. in the guest room, all the cotton products seem to be of good quality; but on the other hand, the toothbrushes and toothpaste , tea-scented three-piece bath soap set, soap hand soap, etc. The hotel's daily chemical products are very watery... The bathing facilities are great, with plenty of hot water and high water pressure, and the cleaning is very clean; the air conditioner starts up effectively , is also very quiet; the guest room TV can watch recent Universal movies (the same as the film list of the Paradise Hotel), in ultra-high definition quality, but the number is quite small and some are in English...
During our stay, we spent most of our time in the park, so we didn‚Äôt have much understanding or experience of the facilities outside the hotel rooms. The hotel has a children‚Äôs playground and swimming pool, as well as a Universal Park souvenir shop. They were all in a hurry. Passing by and taking a glance through the window, everything seemed pretty good.
The hotel's breakfast buffet looks quite rich. Porridge/noodles/wontons + sausages/breads/vegetables are both Chinese and Western. The dishes are very exquisite, and you can also choose noodles for fried eggs... The only drawback is that I think there is only one coffee machine. Ah, you have to queue up to froth milk...
The hotel's most commendable external aspect is its service level. [Passion] is reflected in "helping others" anytime and anywhere, and "Professionalism" is reflected in daily QA ("answering questions"). In addition, the special needs of hotel guests will be met to a certain extent. For example, it happened to be our birthday on the day we checked in, and the room service also specially sent greeting cards (and some balloons...) and quite delicious chocolate cake; after learning that we Next we have to go to the Paradise Hotel next door, and they helped us transfer our luggage directly. We communicated by phone before arriving at the hotel, and we can mention our check-in requirements. A few days after leaving the hotel, the guest relations department will also pay a return visit to ask if there are any deficiencies (the hotel If the boss sees this, please add chicken drumsticks to Miss Guo)
In summary, if you are like us and enter the park in advance every day (you can get two free days if you stay for one night) and return only after the park closes, the Nuo Hotel is not far more convenient than the Paradise Hotel next door. The hotel next door is "next floor + 4 queuing lanes", and the NUO Hotel is "morning exercise + 1 queuing lane". Going back and forth to Universal Avenue after closing is relatively cumbersome. In terms of accommodation conditions and services, NUO Hotel seems to be better (just there are no dolls to interact with...). The accommodation environment is very good, the catering is excellent, the hotel's internal facilities are also very good, and even... There are garden views.

posted:Posted November 19, 2023
msg:Overall, I am very satisfied. I started my vacation in Beijing directly after having dinner with clients on Thursday. As soon as you enter the hotel, there will be a waiter to help you with your luggage and guide you to the front desk.

The front desk skillfully helped me check in and upgraded my room type for free. Informed about free drinks in the minibar and an hour in advance.
Then the waiter guided me to my room. On the way to the room, the service staff introduced me to some of Universal's projects, and finally asked me to search for Beijing Universal's mini program on WeChat. This mini program is very convenient and easy to use. On the way, I noticed that there is an isolation door from the lobby to the guest room area, and you must swipe your card to enter. Therefore, the guest room area is very quiet, with almost no sound of people moving around. The room I stayed in this time was on the second floor, and the front desk was on the third floor, so we went down one floor.

Entering the room, there is a cloakroom and a desk for luggage (the cloakroom is equipped with a safe). It is separated from the bedroom by a wall. When you enter the door and turn left, you will find a separate bathroom with a door, which is quite large. After exiting the bathroom, turn left to reach the bathroom. The bathroom contains a large shower, two mirrors, two sinks and a large bathtub. The curtains of the large bathtub open and you can see the Universal Hotel, which is the main entrance of the studio. It means that Nuojin is not far from the movie theater, and it only takes about five to ten minutes to walk there at night. The bathroom mirror faces the bedroom. Bathroom and bedroom, bathroom and dressing room can be separated by sliding wooden doors.
The body soap, shampoo, conditioner in the shower room, the small soap next to the sink, and the moisturizing lotion next to the bathtub are all Pu'er series of toiletries customized by Nuojin. The toothpaste is imported Colgate, along with a bottle of Listerine mouthwash and a bag of bath salts. Next to the sink is a concave mirror with a ring light for makeup. I didn't notice the brand of the hair dryer, but it was placed on the left side of the sink, together with the anti-slip mat. The bathtub drains water very quickly and the temperature is easily controlled. The shower room is large enough for a family to take a shower at the same time. Perhaps considering family travel, all disposable items are available in children's sizes.

There is a sofa in front of the bed in the bedroom. There is a tea set on the small table in front of the sofa, with four kinds of tea bags. The sofa and bed are facing the TV, which is large and clear. You can watch ten Universal movies for free, as well as regular channels or satellite channels. The office desk is large and equipped with a high-quality backing board. It‚Äôs also convenient to reply to a few urgent emails or handle urgent work during your vacation. On the other side of the TV is a minibar equipped with a capsule coffee machine, a hot water kettle and cups. The capsule coffee comes with two flavors, a total of six cups (the last time I stayed in a hotel with capsule coffee was the Mandarin Oriental in Hong Kong). There are two bottles of mineral water in the minibar refrigerator, one bottle each of Yanjing Beer and Tsingtao Beer, one can of Coca-Cola without sugar and one with sugar, one can of Sprite, and one can of sugar-free soda water. There are also four small bottles of mineral water and a large bottle of mineral water on the minibar, and two bottles of mineral water in the bathroom.

However, I think the biggest advantage of the hotel is to enter the park an hour in advance. With this extra hour, you can finish the two scenic spots first with almost no queues. Projects in other scenic spots can also be participated in when the queue is small. If everything goes well, you can enjoy all the fifteen amu*****t rides around the world in the morning. In the afternoon you can focus on watching shows, small projects or shopping.

Finally, check-out and luggage storage are very convenient, and you don‚Äôt even need to queue at the front desk to check out. The waiter will help process it after getting your room card. When storing my luggage, the service staff would ask for my room number and mobile phone number, but when I actually picked up my luggage, I only used the small card the waiter gave me.

1. Overall: NUO Hotel is overall a**ospheric and simple, with modern decoration, new facilities, bright corridors, and special access control in the guest room area to enhance the sense of space privacy. The hotel staff are very enthusiastic, take the initiative to say hello, help guide the way, and have a strong sense of service. Check-in at the front desk was fast.
2. Dining: There are Xiyue Restaurant and Hejia Restaurant on the first floor of the hotel. Xiyue's breakfast has a wide variety, including Chinese and Western dishes; dinner is a buffet, and supplementary meals such as steak and seafood are fast. Hejia has a good environment, exquisite dishes, and high prices, about 500 per capita. If you don't want to eat in the hotel, you can eat on City Avenue.
3. Entertainment: The hotel has a swimming pool, spa, and gym, all together, very convenient. There is also a play area for children.
4. Guest room: The interior of the room is comfortable, with basic facilities, good sound insulation, and fast room service.
5. Transportation:
       From the small door on the first floor of the hotel, you can directly lead to the city avenue, and you can walk for 3 minutes. There is an exclusive security check channel. When you return, you can go back to the hotel through the security check gate on the same road.
       The gate on the first floor of the hotel can directly lead to the Universal Studios Park. There are staff and road signs to guide you. It takes 5 minutes to walk. You need to bring your ID card (to check the accommodation information) to enter the park through the exclusive channel.
        The hotel parking lot is outsourced and requires a fee of 180 a day. If you take the subway to the hotel, turn right when you get out of the station and follow the sign to walk for 3 minutes.

This experience is good, the child is very happy, and I look forward to coming back another day.

The room is 20 square meters larger than the Universal Studios Hotel. (Both are double beds) The cost is even cheaper than that of the Universal Studios Hotel, about 300~400 per night.

And it must be recommended to order from Ctrip, because it is cheaper than the APP.

The beds are very comfortable, all comfort levels are good, and it's not too far to get to the Universal City Hotel and City Boulevard.

The uncleanness of the kettle is a common problem in all hotels, and this is no exception
